FNV PBR PPLIGHTING INTERFACE RECORD TABLE AUDIT

Questions:
1. Which E7F430 record keys/lists are registered by PPLighting setup functions?
2. Which vtable helpers execute each shader-interface record type class?
3. Which pass-entry helpers map PPLighting branches to concrete pass IDs/resources?
4. Is one replacement family concrete enough to bind a BRDF shader without guessing?

Compatibility rule:
Do not bind a replacement shader until this output yields a per-family record/stage table.
